Highcharts has now been upgraded to version 4 of the API, but this will not work unless an API key is given in the <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/highcharts/data.googleAPIKey\">data.googleAPIKey</a> option. See the <a href=\"https://handsondataviz.org/google-sheets-api-key.html\">comprehensive tutorial</a> from Hands-On Data Visualization on how to obtain the key. Additionally, <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/highcharts/data.googleSpreadsheetWorksheet\">data.googleSpreadsheetWorksheet</a> is deprecated and replaced by <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/highcharts/data.googleSpreadsheetRange\">data.googleSpreadsheetRange</a>, which allows for more detailed instructions on what data to load.</li>\n        </ul>\n\n Highcharts. The <code>chart.panning.type</code> now accepts <code>y</code> directions.</li>\n  <li>Added box options for <code>yAxis.stackLabels</code>: <code>backgroundColor</code>, <code>borderWidth</code>, <code>borderRadius</code> and <code>borderColor</code>. See #13330.</li>\n  <li>Added new series label options, <code>series.label.format</code> and <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/highcharts/plotOptions.series.label.formatter\">series.label.formatter</a>.</li>\n  <li>Added individual dash style settings for various parts of box plots. See #13065.</li>\n  <li>Added language options for export-data table text, see #13166.</li>\n  <li>Added ability to set markers of heatmap points to a custom shapes defined within <code>SVGRenderer.prototype.symbols</code> object, see #12508.</li>\n</ul>\n<div class=\"accordion card-group\">\n  <div class=\"card\">\n    <div id=\"heading-8-1-0-upgrade-notes\" class=\"card-header\">\n      <h4 class=\"card-title\">\n        <button aria-label=\"Upgrade Notes Highcharts v8.1.0\" aria-expanded=\"false\" class=\"btn btn-link collapsed\" type=\"button\" data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-target=\"#upgrade-notes-8-1-0\"><span> Upgrade notes </span></button>\n      </h4>\n    </div>\n    <div id=\"upgrade-notes-8-1-0\" class=\"collapse\" aria-labelledby=\"heading-8-1-0-bug-fixes\" data-parent=\".accordion\">\n      <div class=\"card-body\">\n        <ul>\n          <li>The Axis class was refactored as part of the TypeScript migration. Axis extensions like log axis, broken axis, parallel axis, datetime axis and ordinal axis are now handled as compositions. Instead of adding multiple properties to the main axis instance, they now add a single object that holds all properties. This does not affect the options API, but it may affect implementations that are based on some of our samples that used the original properties. Our samples have been updated to use the new structure.</li>\n          <li>For added type safety, we are now defining SVG path definition as two-dimensional arrays, or in TypeScript sense an array of tuples. So <code>[&#39;M&#39;, 0, 0, &#39;L&#39;, 100, 100]</code> in the new implementation should be written <code>[[&#39;M&#39;, 0, 0], [&#39;L&#39;, 100, 100]]</code>. We built in a converter for old paths, but there may be cases, like for example directly accessing <code>SVGRenderer.crispLine</code>, where it breaks.</li>\n        </ul>\n\n      </div>\n    </div>\n    <div id=\"heading-8-1-0-bug-fixes\" class=\"card-header\">\n      <h4 class=\"card-title\" aria-label=\"Bug Fixes Highcharts v8.1.0\">\n        <button aria-label=\"Bug Fixes Highcharts v8.1.0\" aria-expanded=\"false\" class=\"btn btn-link collapsed\" type=\"button\" data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-target=\"#bug-fixes-8-1-0\"><span> Bug fixes </span></button>\n      </h4>\n    </div>\n    <div id=\"bug-fixes-8-1-0\" class=\"collapse\" aria-labelledby=\"heading-8-1-0-bug-fixes\" data-parent=\".accordion\">\n      <div class=\"card-body\">\n        <ul>\n          <li>Fixed issue with missing accessibility options in the API.</li>\n          <li>Fixed #12767, exported data table had wrong points categories.</li>\n          <li>Fixed #13305, focus border not updated with scrolling points.</li>\n          <li>Fixed #11500, stack labels had a wrong position after moving X axis or Y axis.</li>\n          <li>Fixed #13332, 3D column not working on IE browsers. id=\"highcharts-v7.0.0\"></a>\n  <span>Highcharts v7.0.0 (2018-12-11)</span>\n  <a class=\"release-header-hashtag\" href=\"#highcharts-v7.0.0\">#</a>\n\n</h3>\n<ul>\n  <li>Added <a href=\"https://www.highcharts.com/demo/sonification\">sonification</a> to the accessibility features.</li>\n  <li>Added TypeScript support (Beta).</li>\n  <li>Added <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/highcharts/legend.bubbleLegend\">bubble legends</a>, legend items describing the scale of the bubbles.</li>\n  <li>Added feature to match points by id when running href=\"https://www.highcharts.com/demo/packed-bubble\">packed bubble</a>.</li>\n  <li>Added new series type <a href=\"https://www.highcharts.com/demo/cylinder\">3D cylinder</a>.</li>\n  <li>Added new series type <a href=\"https://www.highcharts.com/demo/venn-diagram\">venn diagram</a>.</li>\n  <li>Added new series type <a href=\"https://www.highcharts.com/demo/column-pyramid\">column pyramid chart</a>.</li>\n  <li>Added editor features for annotations, allowing annotations to be added, updated and removed through a GUI.</li>\n  <li>Added debug module for making chart errors visible in the   <div id=\"upgrade-notes-7-0-0\" class=\"collapse\" aria-labelledby=\"heading-7-0-0-bug-fixes\" data-parent=\".accordion\">\n      <div class=\"card-body\">\n        <ul>\n          <li>If you use styled mode, the setup has changed. Instead of loading files from the <code>code.highcharts.com/js</code> folder, use the base JavaScript files, but set the <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/highcharts/chart.styledMode\">chart.styledMode</a> option to true.</li>\n          <li>Polyfills are now needed for support in IE 6-8. Before including the <code>highcharts.js</code> file, load <code>modules/oldie-polyfills.js</code> in a conditional comment. Alternatively you can use your own polyfills or a third party library. See <a href=\"https://www.highcharts.com/docs/getting-started/system-requirements#oldie\">System Requirements</a>.</li>\n          <li>If the <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/highcharts/chart.height\">chart.height</a> setting is higher than the CSS height of the container, the chart will now be clipped. This is a consequence of adapting the chart to table cells and flex layouts.</li>\n        </ul>\n\n      </div>\n    </div>\n    <div id=\"heading-7-0-0-bug-fixes\" class=\"card-header\">\n      <h4 class=\"card-title\" aria-label=\"Bug Fixes Highcharts v7.0.0\">\n        <button aria-label=\"Bug Fixes Highcharts v7.0.0\" aria-expanded=\"false\" class=\"btn btn-link collapsed\" type=\"button\" data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-target=\"#bug-fixes-7-0-0\"><span> Bug fixes </span></button>\n      </h4>\n    </div>\n    <div id=\"bug-fixes-7-0-0\" class=\"collapse\" aria-labelledby=\"heading-7-0-0-bug-fixes\" data-parent=\".accordion\">\n      <div class=\"card-body\">\n        <ul>\n          <li>Corrected chart width for sub-pixel container width. (2015-02-16)</span>\n  <a class=\"release-header-hashtag\" href=\"#highcharts-v4.1.0\">#</a>\n\n</h3>\n<ul>\n  <li>Added <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/#plotOptions.polygon\">polygon</a> series type.</li>\n  <li>Added <code>e.category</code> event argument in drilldown events to make it clear when a category is clicked. Related to #3771.</li>\n  <li>Added new option to the data module, <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/#data.firstRowAsNames\">firstRowAsNames</a>.</li>\n  <li>Added new option, <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/#plotOptions.series.pointIntervalUnit\">pointIntervalUnit</a>, in order to allow months and years as point intervals. Closes #3329.</li>\n  <li>Added <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/#chart.events.beforePrint\">beforePrint</a> and <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/#chart.events.afterPrint\">afterPrint</a> events. Related to #2284 and #3729.</li>\n  <li>Added new method, <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/#Series.removePoint\">Series.removePoint</a>, to allow removing points that are not instanciated on demand.</li>\n  <li>Added new option, global.getTimezoneOffset, to allow integration with third party timezone libraries like moment-timezone.js.</li>\n  <li>Added new Axis option, <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/#yAxis.tickAmount\">tickAmount</a>. Refactored alignTicks on multi-axis charts to first compute a <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/#yAxis.tickAmount\">tickAmount</a>, then make all axes comply with that.</li>\n  <li>Added new Axis option, <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/#xAxis.labels.autoRotation\">autoRotation</a> as an array of possible values.</li>\n  <li>Added new callback option, <a href=\"https://api.highcharts.com/#tooltip.pointFormatter\">tooltip.pointFormatter</a>.</li>\n  <li>Added polar support for arearange. Issue #3419.</li>\n  <li>In solid gauges, added support for initial animation as well as setting animation object for updates. Closes #3135.</li>\n  <li>Made the entire numberFormat method settable and wrappable from the outside.</li>\n  <li>Made tooltip.followTouchMove true by default, and allowed page scroll at the same time.</li>\n  <li>Implemented support for &quot;contrast&quot; color setting in data labels. When the data label is inside a shape (like a column), this will ensure the best readability.</li>\n  <li>On category axes, let the crosshair width cover the whole category like a band.</li>\n  <li>Refactored zIndex handling on SVGElements so that the zIndex can also be modified after the element is first added.</li>\n  <li>Changed the Axis.tickPositioner callback so that the default tick positioning logic runs first, to allow modification in the tick positioner instead of creating positions from scratch. Closes #3538.</li>\n  <li>Made the legend draw below or above the plot area in cases where it is placed in a corner and the layout is horizontal.</li>\n  <li>Implemented algorithm for setting precise tooltip xDateFormat when needed, but general format like year, month, day etc. when the time falls on midnight and the closest point range dictates it. Related to #3329.</li>\n  <li>New default behaviour for the xAxis.minTickInterval option on datetime axis. It now goes to the closest point range by default.</li>\n  <li>Implemented silent degradation instead of error 19 when user options dictate too many ticks on an axis.</li>\n  <li>Removed overflow:justify logic. Instead, move labels and add ellipsis in case of overflow.</li>\n  <li>Export server: Adapted to PhantomJS 2.</li>\n  <li>Export server: Implemented XSS filter.</li>\n  <li>Fixed error on applying stacking to area range series.</li>\n  <li>Partly fixed #3506, overlapping axis labels on polar chart.</li>\n  <li>Fixed waterfall issue where the upColor stayed after updating point to negative. collapsed\" type=\"button\" data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-target=\"#upgrade-notes-2-1-0\"><span> Upgrade notes </span></button>\n      </h4>\n    </div>\n    <div id=\"upgrade-notes-2-1-0\" class=\"collapse\" aria-labelledby=\"heading-2-1-0-bug-fixes\" data-parent=\".accordion\">\n      <div class=\"card-body\">\n        <ul>\n          <li>Legend positioning: Since version 2.1 Highcharts is aware of the size of the titles and legend and will try to make room for these in the chart&#39;s margins. When upgrading from older versions, this may lead to too great margins depending on where your legend is positioned. To prevent this, set a new option, floating to true in your legend options. Furthermore, the x and y values of the legend position is now relative to the chart.spacingTop and chart.spacingLeft etc. properties instead of the chart&#39;s outer edge.</li>\n        </ul>\n\n      </div>\n    </div>\n    <div id=\"heading-2-1-0-bug-fixes\" class=\"card-header\">\n      <h4 class=\"card-title\" aria-label=\"Bug Fixes Highcharts v2.1.0\">\n        <button aria-label=\"Bug Fixes Highcharts v2.1.0\" aria-expanded=\"false\" class=\"btn btn-link collapsed\" type=\"button\" data-toggle=\"collapse\" data-target=\"#bug-fixes-2-1-0\"><span> Bug fixes </span></button>\n      </h4>\n    </div>\n    <div id=\"bug-fixes-2-1-0\" class=\"collapse\" aria-labelledby=\"heading-2-1-0-bug-fixes\" data-parent=\".accordion\">\n      <div class=\"card-body\">\n        <ul>\n          <li>Fixed bugs as listed at <a href=\"https://github.com/highcharts/highcharts/commits/master\">GitHub</a> under dates since the last maintenance version.</li>\n        </ul>\n\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  </div>\n</div>\n<h3 class=\"release-header\">\n  <a id=\"highcharts-v2.0.5\"></a>\n  <span>Highcharts v2.0.5 (2010-09-17)</span>\n  <a class=\"release-header-hashtag\" href=\"#highcharts-v2.0.5\">#</a>\n\n</h3>\n<ul>\n  <li>Optimized for IE9 Beta 1.
